A macro is a sequence of one or more requests. You can use macros within session handling rules to perform tasks such as logging in to the application, obtaining anti-CSRF tokens, etc.	宏是一个或多个请求的序列。使用会话处理规则中的宏，您可以执行任务，例如登录应用程序或获取CSRF对策令牌。
A macro is a sequence of one or more requests. You can use macros within session handling rules to perform tasks such as logging in to the application, obtaining anti-CSRF tokens, etc. Use these settings to manage your macros.	一个宏是一个或多个请求的序列。你可以在会话处理规则中使用宏来执行任务，如登录到应用程序，获得反CSRF令牌等。使用这些设置来管理你的宏。

A resource pool is a grouping of tasks that share a quota of network resources. Each resource pool can be configured with its own throttling settings which control the number of requests that can be made concurrently, or the rate at which requests can be made, or both.	资源池对共享网络资源分配的任务进行了分组。每个资源池都可以设置为调整同时请求的数量或请求的速度或两者。
A resource pool is a grouping of tasks that share a quota of network resources. Each resource pool can have its own throttling settings, controlling the number of concurrent requests that can be made, the rate at which those requests can be made, or both.	一个资源池是一组共享网络资源配额的任务。每个资源池都可以有自己的节流设置，控制可以发出的并发请求的数量，可以发出这些请求的速度，或者两者都有。

All bits failed the test. 	全部bits测试失败。 
All bits passed the test. 	全部bits测试合格。 
All bits passed the test. Note that the FIPS specification for this test only records a fail if the longest run of bits is overly long. However, an overly short longest run of bits also indicates that the sample is not random. Therefore some bits may record a significance level that is below the FIPS pass level even though they do not strictly fail the FIPS test.	全部bits测试合格。请注意，在此测试的FIPS规范中，只有当bits的最长连太长时，才会失败。然而，太短bits的最长连续也表明样本不是随机的。因此，某些bits可能低于FIPS合格水平，尽管未通过严格的FIPS测试。

Crawler Settings	爬行设置
Crawling	爬行
Crawling modern applications is sometimes an open-ended exercise, due to the amount of stateful functionality, volatile content, and unbounded navigation. Burp's crawler uses various techniques to maximise discovery of unique content early in the crawl. These settings let you impose a limit on the extent of the crawl, as it reaches the point of diminishing returns. You can leave any crawl limit setting blank to disable it.	由于有状态的功能，不稳定的内容和无限的导航，最新的应用爬行可能是无止境的。Burp爬虫使用不同的方法，试图在爬行的早期阶段最大限度地发现独特的内容。这些设置会限制爬行范围。将爬行限制保留为空白，即可禁用。

Scan configuration	扫描设置
Scan configurations and modes are groups of settings that define how a scan is performed. Scan modes offer preset options designed to let you trade off speed and coverage. Alternatively, you can select one or more custom configurations. Burp Scanner applies any selected configurations in order, enabling you to fine-tune scanning behaviour.	扫描配置和模式是定义如何进行扫描的一组设置。扫描模式提供了预设的选项，旨在让你在速度和覆盖范围之间进行权衡。或者，您可以选择一个或多个自定义配置。Burp扫描器按顺序应用任何选定的配置，使您能够微调扫描行为。

The chart shows the maximum bits of entropy available at each position, given the size of the character set used at that position. The total amount of possible entropy is ([.0-9]+) bits.	该图显示了每个位置的熵的最大位，由该位置使用的字符集的大小给出。有效熵的总数如下$1位。
The chart shows the number of bits of effective entropy at each significance level, based on all tests. Each significance level defines a minimum probability of the observed results occurring if the sample is randomly generated. When the probability of the observed results occurring falls below this level, the hypothesis that the sample is randomly generated is rejected. Using a lower significance level means that stronger evidence is required to reject the hypothesis that the sample is random, and so increases the chance that non-random data will be treated as random.	该图显示了基于所有测试的有效熵比特数与每个显著水平。每个显著水平定义了当样本随机生成时发生的观测结果的最小概率。如果观察结果的概率低于此水平，则假设样本是随机生成的。降低显著水平需要更强大的证据来否定随机生成令牌的假设，从而增加了非随机数据被视为随机的可能性。
The chart shows the number of bits of effective entropy at each significance level, based on the bit-level tests. Each significance level defines a minimum probability of the observed results occurring if the sample is randomly generated. When the probability of the observed results occurring falls below this level, the hypothesis that the sample is randomly generated is rejected. Using a lower significance level means that stronger evidence is required to reject the hypothesis that the sample is random, and so increases the chance that non-random data will be treated as random.	该图显示了基于比特水平测试的每个显著水平的有效熵比特数。每个显著水平定义了当样本随机生成时发生的观测结果的最小概率。如果观察结果的概率低于此水平，则假设样本是随机生成的。降低显著水平需要更强大的证据来否定随机生成令牌的假设，从而增加了非随机数据被视为随机的可能性。

This payload type can be used to generate illegal Unicode representations of characters. It is sometimes effective in bypassing filters designed to block certain characters. See the full help for details of each option.	生成非法Unicode符号的字符串。这可能有助于避免过滤器被设计为阻止特定字符。有关每个选项的详细信息，请参阅帮助。
This payload type can be used to shuffle blocks of ciphertext in ECB-encrypted data, so as to meaningfully modify the decrypted cleartext and potentially interfere with application logic. You can optionally supply a list of encrypted strings that use the same cipher and key, to provide additional blocks for shuffling into the original data.	重新排列ECB加密数据的密文块可能会在解密时变成有意义的明文，并导致应用逻辑变得不稳定。如果需要，您可以使用相同的加密和密钥指定加密字符串的列表，并将其用作原始数据中的混洗附加块。
This payload type copies the value of the current payload at another payload position. It can be used with attack types that have multiple payload sets.	该有效载荷类型将另一个有效载荷的值复制到当前有效载荷值。可用于使用多个有效载荷集的攻击类型。

This strategy applies some optimizations to the coverage of the crawl, with some loss of speed in some applications. It is appropriate for applications with volatile or overloaded URLs, or more complex stateful functionality than normal.	该策略对抓取的完整性应用了一些优化，但在某些应用中会失去速度。它适用于挥发性或高负载URL应用程序，以及具有比通常更复杂的状态功能的应用程序。
This strategy applies some optimizations to the speed of the crawl, with some loss of coverage in some applications. It is appropriate for applications that use mostly stable and unique URLs, and only limited or simple stateful functionality.	该策略对抓取速度应用了一些优化，但在某些应用中失去了完整性。适用于大多数独特、稳定且只有有限或简单的有状态功能的情况。
This strategy optimizes as far as possible for the coverage of the crawl, at the expense of speed in most applications. It is appropriate to achieve strong coverage of applications with highly volatile or overloaded URLs or heavily complex stateful functionality.	该策略尽可能优化抓取的完整性，但在大多数应用中速度都会降低。适用于高挥发性网址和高负载网址，以及强大覆盖非常复杂的有状态功能的情况。
This strategy optimizes as far as possible for the speed of the crawl, at the expense of lower coverage in many applications. It is appropriate for applications with stable and unique URLs, and no stateful functionality (e.g. authentication). Cookies from the Cookie Jar will be used as initial values.	这种策略尽可能地优化了爬行的速度，在许多应用中以降低覆盖率为代价。它适合于具有稳定和独特的URL，并且没有状态功能（如认证）的应用程序。Cookie Jar中的Cookie将被用作初始值。
This strategy optimizes as far as possible for the speed of the crawl, at the expense of lower coverage in many applications. It is appropriate for applications with stable and unique URLs, and no stateful functionality.	该策略尽可能优化爬行速度，但在许多应用中降低了完整性。适用于URL独特、稳定且无状态功能的应用程序。
This strategy represents a trade-off between coverage and speed that is appropriate for typical applications.	该策略在一般应用中实现了全面和速度的平衡。
This test analyzes the distribution of characters used at each position within the token. If the sample is randomly generated, the distribution of characters employed is likely to be approximately uniform. At each position, the test computes the probability of the observed distribution arising if the tokens are random. The significance level at each position is the probability of the observed distribution of characters occurring, assuming that the sample is randomly generated.	分析标记中每个位置使用的字符分布。如果样本是随机生成的，则使用的字符分布应该基本均匀。在此测试中，我们将计算每个位置的分布概率，如果令牌是随机的，则应该观察到。如果假设样本是随机生成的，则每个位置的显著水平是观察到发生的字符分布的概率。
This test analyzes the distribution of ones and zeroes at each bit position. If the sample is randomly generated, the number of ones and zeroes is likely to be approximately equal. At each position, the test computes the probability of the observed distribution arising if the tokens are random. The significance level at each position is the probability of the observed number of ones and zeroes occurring, assuming that the sample is randomly generated.	分析1和0在每个位位置的分布。如果样本是随机生成的，那么1和0的分布应该几乎是均匀的。在此测试中，我们将计算每个位置的分布概率，如果令牌是随机的，则应该观察到。如果假设样本是随机生成的，则每个位置的显著水平是观察到0和1发生的数量的概率。
This test analyzes the relationships between bits at different positions within the token. If the sample is randomly generated, a value at a given bit position is equally likely to be accompanied by a one or a zero at any other bit position. At each position, the test computes the probability of the relationships observed with bits at other positions arising if the tokens are random. To prevent arbitrary results, when a degree of correlation is observed between two bits, the test adjusts the significance level of the bit whose significance level is lower based on all of the other bit-level tests.	此测试分析令牌中不同位置的位之间的关系。如果样本是随机生成的，则特定位的值应该与其他位位置变为0或1的概率大致相等。测试计算在每个位置，如果令牌是随机的，所观察到的其他位置的位的概率。如果观察到2位之间的相关性，以防止任意结果，其他位电平测试调整位显著水平较低的位的显著水平。
This test analyzes the transitions between successive tokens in the sample. If the sample is randomly generated, a character appearing at a given position is equally likely to be followed in the next token by any one of the characters that is used at that position. At each position, the test computes the probability of the observed transitions arising if the tokens are random. The significance level at each position is the probability of the observed transitions occurring, assuming that the sample is randomly generated.	分析样品中连续令牌之间的过渡。如果样本是随机生成的，那么对于出现在某个位置的字符，无论过去在相同位置使用的字符是什么，在下一个令牌中也出现在相同位置的概率应该是相同的。在此测试中，我们将计算每个位置的迁移概率，如果令牌是随机的，则应该观察到。每个位置的显著水平是在假设样本是随机生成的情况下，观察到发生的过渡的概率。
This test attempts to compress the bit sequence at each position using standard ZLIB compression. The results indicate the proportional reduction in the size of the bit sequence when it was compressed. A higher degree of compression indicates that the data is less likely to be randomly generated.	此测试尝试使用标准ZLIB压缩压缩每个位置的位串。压缩后，位串的大小会按比例减小。高压缩比表示数据不是随机生成的。
This test divides the bit sequence at each position into consecutive, non-overlapping groups of four, and derives a four-bit number from each group. It then counts the number of occurrences of each of the 16 possible numbers, and performs a chi-square calculation to evaluate this distribution. If the sample is randomly generated, the distribution of four-bit numbers is likely to be approximately uniform. At each position, the test computes the probability of the observed distribution arising if the tokens are random. The significance level at each position is the probability of the observed distribution occurring, assuming that the sample is randomly generated.	将每个位置的位串分成四个连续的非重复组，并从每个组中导出4位的值。接下来，计算可能出现的16个数字的出现次数，并计算卡方以评估此分布。如果样本是随机生成的，那么4位数值的分布应该几乎是均匀的。在此测试中，我们将计算每个位置的分布概率，如果令牌是随机的，则应该观察到。假设样本是随机的，每个位置的显著水平是观察到的分布发生的概率。
This test divides the bit sequence at each position into runs of consecutive bits which have the same value. It then counts the number of runs with a length of 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, and 6 and above. If the sample is randomly generated, the number of runs with each of these lengths is likely to be within a range determined by the size of the sample set. At each position, the test computes the probability of the observed runs occurring if the tokens are random. The significance level at each position is the probability of the observed runs occurring, assuming that the sample is randomly generated.	此测试将每个位置的位串划分为具有相同值的连续位。然后数长度为1，2，3，4，5，6，甚至更长的连的数量。如果样本是随机生成的，则每个长度的序列的数量应该大致落在由样本集的大小确定的范围内。？在此测试中，我们将计算每个位置的连续概率，在随机情况下可以观察到令牌。假设样本是随机的，每个位置的显著水平是观察到的通信发生的概率。
This test measures the longest run of bits with the same value at each bit position. If the sample is randomly generated, the longest run is likely to be within a range determined by the size of the sample set. At each position, the test computes the probability of the observed longest run arising if the tokens are random. The significance level at each position is the probability of the observed longest run occurring, assuming that the sample is randomly generated.	在每个位位置测量具有相同值的位的最长连续。如果样本是随机生成的，则最长连续应该大致在由样本集的大小确定的范围内。在此测试中，对于每个位置，计算在令牌是随机的情况下应该观察到的最长通信概率。假设样本是随机的，每个位置的显著水平是观察到的最长通信发生的概率。
This test performs a sophisticated analysis of the bit sequence at each position, and is capable of identifying evidence of non-randomness in some samples which pass the other statistical tests. The test works through the bit sequence and treats each series of consecutive numbers as coordinates in a multi-dimensional space. It plots a point in this space at each location determined by these co-ordinates. If the sample is randomly generated, the distribution of points within this space is likely to be approximately uniform; the appearance of clusters within the space indicates that the data is likely to be non-random. At each position, the test computes the probability of the observed distribution occurring if the tokens are random. The test is repeated for multiple sizes of number (between 1 and 8 bits) and for multiple numbers of dimensions (between 2 and 6). The significance level at each position is the probability of the observed results occurring, assuming that the sample is randomly generated.	此测试可以执行对每个位置的位序列的高级分析，并发现通过其他统计测试的一些样本的非随机性证据。该测试处理比特串，并将一系列连续的数字视为多维空间的坐标。绘制由这些坐标确定的每个位置的空间中的点。如果样本是随机生成的，那么这个空间中的点分布应该几乎是均匀的；如果空间内出现偏差，数据很可能不是随机的。在此测试中，我们将针对每个位置计算分布的发生概率，在随机情况下可以观察到令牌。此测试在多个维度(2到6)中重复，包括多个大小(1到8位)的数量。如果假设样本是随机的，每个位置的显著水平是观察到的结果发生的概率。

Warning: changes will not be applied	注意: 更改不适用。
Warning: The CSRF form uses a different encoding type than the original request, and so the application may not process the request in the way required.	警告: CSRF表单使用与原始请求不同的编码，因此应用程序可能无法以指定的方式处理请求。
Warning: The XmlHttpRequest technique only works on modern browsers, and the browser will not display the response to the CSRF request. The request contains some non-standard headers which, if included in a cross-domain XHR, may cause the request to be pre-flighted, and so the attack may fail. These headers have been omitted in the PoC attack, to avoid pre-flighting. If the omitted headers are essential for the efficacy of the CSRF attack, you can manually add these to the PoC HTML.	警告: XmlHttpRequest方法仅适用于最新的浏览器，浏览器不显示CSRF请求的响应。如果跨域XHR中的请求包含非标准标头，则可能会发生预飞请求，并且攻击可能会失败。为了避免预飞行，省略了这些标题。如果省略了有效CSRF攻击的标题是必不可少的，则可以手动将其添加到PoC HTML中。
Warning: The XmlHttpRequest technique only works on modern browsers, and the browser will not display the response to the CSRF request. The request contains some non-standard headers which, if included in a cross-domain XHR, may cause the request to be pre-flighted, and so the attack may fail. These headers have been omitted in the PoC attack, to avoid pre-flighting. If the omitted headers are essential for the efficacy of the CSRF attack, you can manually add these to the PoC HTML. The request includes a Content-Type header with a non-standard value, which may cause the request to be pre-flighted, and so the attack may fail. If the non-standard header is not essential for the efficacy of the CSRF attack, you can try using a standard value in the Content-Type header instead.	警告: XmlHttpRequest方法仅适用于最新的浏览器，浏览器不显示CSRF请求的响应。如果跨域XHR中的请求包含非标准标头，则可能会发生预飞请求，并且攻击可能会失败。为了避免预飞行，省略了这些标题。如果省略了有效CSRF攻击的标题是必不可少的，则可以手动将其添加到PoC HTML中。由于请求具有非标准值的Content-Type头，因此可能会发生预飞请求，攻击可能会失败。如果非标准标头不是CSRF攻击所必需的，请尝试使用标准Content-Type标头，而不是使用标准Content-Type标头。
Warning: this also removes any extensions that you have installed.	警告：这还会删除您已安装的所有扩展。
Warning: This tracer imposes a processing and storage overhead, and should only be used when troubleshooting issues with session handling rules.	警告:该示踪器会对处理和存储造成负担，因此只应用于会话处理规则的故障排除。

We recommend that you only have one current project per Collaborator identifier, in order to prevent interference between instances of Burp. As such, you should only include the identifier in your project if you plan to resume testing later, or if you want to pass the project to someone else to take over your testing.	我们建议每个协作者标识符只能有一个当前项目，以防止Burp实例之间的干扰。因此，只有当你打算以后恢复测试，或者你想把项目传给其他人接管你的测试时，你才应该在你的项目中包括这个标识符。

You can define session handling rules to make Burp perform specific actions when making HTTP requests. Each rule has a defined scope (for particular tools, URLs or parameters), and can perform actions such as adding session cookies, logging in to the application, or checking session validity. Before each request is issued, Burp applies in sequence each of the rules that are in-scope for the request.	定义会话处理规则，以执行生成HTTP请求时指定的操作。每个规则定义范围(特定工具、URL、参数)、执行操作(例如添加会话cookie)、登录应用程序和检查会话有效性等。在发出每个请求之前，将每个规则按顺序应用于范围中的请求。
You can define session handling rules to make Burp perform specific actions when making HTTP requests. Each rule has a defined scope (for particular tools, URLs or parameters), and can perform actions such as adding session cookies, logging in to the application, or checking session validity. Before each request is issued, Burp applies in sequence each of the rules that are in-scope for the request. Use these settings to manage your active session handling rules.	你可以定义会话处理规则，使Burp在进行HTTP请求时执行特定的动作。每个规则都有一个定义的范围（针对特定的工具、URL或参数），并且可以执行诸如添加会话cookie、登录到应用程序或检查会话有效性的动作。在每个请求发出之前，Burp会依次应用该请求范围内的每个规则。使用这些设置来管理你的活动会话处理规则。
